<H>{@sūcīpatra
<>svargārohaṇa parba
<>biṣaẏa pr̥ṣṭhāṅka@}
<P>1| prajāṅkaṭhāru yudhiṣṭhiṅkara bidāẏa,
<>parīkṣitaṅku rājanīti śikṣā, subarṇṇa cūḍi
<>o kaḷiyuga bibaraṇa ... 1
<P>2| suhāṇī kanyā śikhareśvara śiba
<>sebāre niyukta gaurī gopāḷuṇī
<>beśe kr̥ttibāsa o kīrttibāsa daityaṅka
<>saṁhāra ... 30
<P>3| yudhiṣṭhiraṅkara uttara diga tīrthe gamana,
<>apratiṣṭhā ḍākeśvarī bibaraṇa,
<>astraśastrādi tyāga ... 43
<P>4| himabanta parbate draupadī, sahadeba,
<>nakuḷa, arjuna o bhīmaṅkara tanutyāga ... 55
<P>5| yudhiṣṭhiraṅkara narka darśana o chaẏāṇoi
<>sahasra rājāṅkara mukti ... 74
<P>6| śvāna rūpe dharmaṅkara prabeśa,
<>yudhiṣṭhiraṅkara indraṅku staba, byāghra
<>darśana o kaḷiyugara niryyātanā ... 76
<P>7| yudhiṣṭhiraṅkara dharma parīkṣā o svaśarīre
<>svarga gamana ... 88
<P>8| pariśiṣṭa ... 98
<P>9| saṁkṣipta mahābhārata ... 101
[MBO-11(3)-1]
<P>{@sāraḷā mahābhārata
<>svargārohaṇa parba
<>prajāṅkaṭhāru yudhiṣṭhiraṅkara bidāẏa,
<>parīkṣitaṅku rājanīti śikṣā,
<>subarṇṇa cuṛi o kaḷiyuga bibaraṇa@}
<P>ẏethu anantare baibasuta manu rājā
<P>agasti muniṁka caraṇe kalāka dibya pūjā | 1 |
<P>aśvamedha yāga kr̥ṣṇa svargārohaṇa uttāreṇa kathā
<P>kahibā bho ruṣi mote pāṇḍabaṁka byabasthā | 2 |
<P1>prathama dhāḍire nimnalikhita bhinma bhinma pothire bhinma pāṭha :--
<P1>ẏethu anantare bilaṁka deśa rājā
<P1>agastiṁka padmapāde kale dibya pūjā |
<P1>nistarili muni tumbhara bākya śuṇi
<P1>ẏethu anantare kathāẏe kaha brahmamuni |
<P1>bauda rūpe kr̥ṣṇa nīḷagirire bijekaḷe
<P1>tahuṁṇa pāṇḍaba ye kebaṇa kr̥tya kale |+
<P1>badanti agasti śuṇimā brahmamuni
<P1>yujheṣṭhi debe rājya pūjā gheni |
<P1>aneka āẏojana ye ratnamāna dile
<P1>samasta rājya prajāṁku binoẏī kahile |
<P1>agasti bolanti śuṇa bilaṁka nr̥pamaṇi
<P1>ẏethu anantare śuṇa svargārohaṇa bāṇī | �ṭa, jha, cha� pothi
[MBO-11(3)-2]
<P>agasti boile ho sābadhāne śuṇa
<P>mahābhāratha ante ye svarga ārohaṇa | 3 |
<P>kathaẏanti mahātamā agasti yurāṇa brahmaruṣi
<P>kaḷiyuga prabeśa ye hoilāka āsi | 4 |
<P>anīti gati loke hele garuhaṁsī
<P>kaḷiyuga siddha ye abhaẏe somabaṁśī | 5 |
<P>driyodhana māri rājya kale kaḷiyugara madhye
<P>āṭhaśata baraṣa helā ẏeṇe kr̥ṣṇa gale badhe | 6 |
<P>kr̥ṣṇara galā uttāre baraṣa śata dui
<P>rājya karuchanti ye pāṇḍaba pāñchabhai | 7 |
<P>ẏe kṣetra mahībhāra rājyara sampada
<P>kesaneka yujheṣthi kale bana sadha | 8 |
<P>kaha mahāmuni mote svarga ārohaṇa bāṇī
<P>agasti boile ho śuṇa nr̥pamaṇi | 9 |
<P>rātra prabhāteṇa āstāne bijaẏe daṇḍadhārī
<P>yujheṣṭhi debe sakaḷa jananta hakāri | 10 |
<P>pātra mantrī amanātya sanya ye prohita
<P>rāiṇa bacana ye bolanti dharmasuta | 11 |
<P>bābu tumbhe sakaḷa jane śuṇimā mora bāṇī
<P>āmbhaṁku sakhā thile deba catrapāṇi | 12 |
<P>kr̥ṣṇara abhābe āmbhaera kisa rājya
<P>kahai tumbhanta yebe āmbhara pūrba kāryya | 13 |
<P>yeteka doṣa tumbhanta achai kari
<P>kṣamā karibāka ẏebe se doṣa mohori | 14 |
<P>mohora apamāna pāila bahuta
<P>ẏe doṣa mohora kṣamā karibā samasta | 15 |
<P1>8|2 yesaneke yujheṣṭhi bacana paramāda |(ka)
[MBO-11(3)-3]
<P>samasta doṣa mora karibā upekṣā
<P>kiñchita puṇye mor abahuta dharma bāñcchā | 16 |
<P>mahatva prāṇīmāne na ghenanti doṣa
<P>kiñchita loke ye bujhanti biśeṣa | 17 |
<P>mote ājahuṁ tumbhe upekṣā karibā
<P>paboṅgkṣa anumate sakaḷe rahibā | 18 |
<P>candreṇa yesane aṭai tārā ye bidita
<P>tesaneka hoi nare tumbhara niẏata | 19 |
<P>ẏe mohora lakṣmī yebe parīkṣaku dei
<P>baneṇa gamana karibuṁ pañchu bhāi | 20 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi bacana śuṇi samasta bismaẏa mana
<P>āmbhanta chaḍi nr̥pati kāhiṁki karibu gabana | 21 |
<P>āmbhe bane yāi samaste tumbhanta karibuṁ sebā
<P>anurāga keteka achai āgyāṁ debā | 22 |
<P>badaẏanti yujheṣṭhi nirmaḷa ẏehu bāṇī
<P>rājya kara tumbhe parīkṣaku gheni | 23 |
<P>mote yete bhagati parīkṣaku debā
<P>tāhāra yete doṣa kale mote upekṣibā | 24 |
<P>parīkṣaku rājya dile hastinā nagarī
<P>pañchu kaṭaka madhye ẏekāṅga daṇḍadhārī | 25 |
<P>pātra br̥hasena mantrī somadāsa
<P>rājyara subidhāna karanti sarba yaśa | 26 |
<P>parīkṣaku tiāranti deba dharma śiṣe
<P>bābu prajā pāḷile barddhuta hoai yaśaśrī āẏuṣe | 27 |
<P1>27|2 parajāṁku yeuṁ rājā pāḷaiṭi dharme
<>ariṣṭhi abidhi na thāi deba dharme |[abaśiṣṭāṁśa para pr̥ṣṭhāre]
[MBO-11(3)-4]
<P>parajāku yebaṇa rājā pāḷai putra tule
<P>deba indra tahim pāḷaiṭi bhale | 28 |
<P>rājā pāḷile se parajā hoi susta
<P>prajā pāḷane kr̥ṣi upujai bahuta | 29 |
<P>kr̥ṣi upujile bhaṇḍāra hoẏe puṣṭa
<P>jaḷa jantumāne na pābanti kaṣṭa | 30 |
<P>āpaṇe śrīkare māpile yujheṣṭhi
<P>aṣṭādaśa hātha hoilā naḷakāṭhi | 31 |
<P>dīrgha pañchabiṁśa prati pañchabiṁśa naḷa uṭhi
<P>ẏemanta ghana karante hoiba ẏeka bāṭi | 32 |
<P>ẏethaku kara bhiāṇa kale seṭi
<P>bāṭikare saṁjā ghenima ẏeka ye pauṭi | 33 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi debe kahile rājyara bidhāna
<P>yatane kahile samasta rājyara subidhāna kathāmāna | 34 |
<P>sujana dekhile niyoga deuthibu
<P>jība thibāyāẏe tāhāku na huḍibu | 35 |
<P>tāhāra antare debu puaku adhikāra
<P>yujheṣṭhi deba tiārile aneka bebhāra | 36 |
<P>saṁcapi kahile ye aneka bidhāna
<P>antakari pāribā ki paṭhana lekhana | 37 |
<P>ẏemantara samaẏe baitaraṇī nadī kūḷe
<P>bedapura boli ye nagra parimaḷe | 38 |
<P1>[pūrba pr̥ṣṭhāra pāṭhāntara]
<P1>parajāṁku yebaṇa rājā pāḷai samatule
<P1>deba indra se rājye pāḷai jāṇa bhale |(cha)
<P1>28|2 kṣetara taṭaku kara ẏeka tule |(ka, ṭa, jha, cha, ḍa)
[MBO-11(3)-5]
<P>se nagre sureśvara boliṇa brāhmaṇa
<P>ẏekadine prabeśa hoile kurṣi karmeṇa | 39 |
<P>taḍapā boliṇa tāhāra kiriṣāṇa
<P>laṅgaḷa gheniṇa se bhūmi karai karaṣaṇa | 40 |
<P>laṅgaḷa pheḍilā uttāre paṇḍāẏe dileka kodāḷa
<P>khetara ṭikara khāla kar asamatula | 41 |
<P>ẏe budā hāṇiṇa tu pākāa bhūmiki
<P>kheta sampūrṇṇa hou bhūmi hou niki | 42 |
<P>āgyāṁ dei bidujana galā nija pure
<P>khḷāi kiriṣāṇa budāi pakāi dūre dūre | 43 |
<P>hāṇante pāṣāṇe yāi bājilāka koḍi
<P>pathara kāḍhante pāilāka ratna jāli | 44 |
<P>dhana dekhiṇa se mahābaḷabantā
<P>mathāre ghenilā se duguṇa śakatā | 45 |
<P>muṇḍiai paṇḍāṁka chamure beta dei
<P>paṇḍāẏe boile nia yā tohora gharakaiṁ | 46 |
<P>kr̥ṣi se āmbhara nā aṭai yugate
<P>karme se yebe pāilu bebhāra aṭai tote | 47 |
<P>bolai taḍāpā gosāiṁ kahila anīti
<P>tumbhara toṭā bāstu tumbhara bāḍibr̥tti | 48 |
<P>tumbhara upara baṁśe kebaṇa sādheba
<P>gupate thoilā āna ke hariba | 49 |
<P>muhiṁ kr̥ṣikārī upujāibi bitta
<P>dhana mohora kisa mūlyahiṁ yugata | 50 |
<P>anna basra barttana huai yete mote
<P>tumbhra āẏe bitta muṁ nemaiṁ kemante | 51 |
<P1>40|2 kiriṣāṇa = kr̥ṣāṇa |
<P1>42|2 niki = bhala |
<P1>44|2 pathara kādhante pāilā ratna jhāli (pāilā ratnatuḍi)(ṇa)
<P1>51|2 tumbhara āẏe bitta = tumbhara se bitta |
[MBO-11(3)-6]
<P>brāhmaṇa bolai tuho śuṇasi sampāda
<P>kr̥ṣāṇa hoi mote karai apabāda | 52 |
<P>ẏehāra karme se upujilā bitta
<P>muhiṁ ẏehā kesaneke karibi grāhita | 53 |
<P>kiriṣāṇa boilā tumbhe puṇyabanta jana
<P>ẏeteka chanda bandha se tumbhara baḍapaṇa | 54 |
<P>bāra cinā barttane anna basre muṁ kāreṇi
<P>rājāra chamure yāiṁ guhāri karibi ẏehikṣaṇi | 55 |
<P>brāhmaṇa boilā bege mathāre ghena ẏehā
<P>rājāra chamuku yibā chālare dorehā | 56 |
<P>āho caitana brāhmaṇa kariṣāṇa duhiṁkara kaḷi
<P>dhana gheni duheṁ yujheṣṭhi debaṁka chamure yāiṁ miḷi | 57 |
<P>siṁghadvāre nei thoileka nidhi
<P>kiriṣāṇa boilā mote hoilā abidhi | 58 |
<P>brāhmaṇa boilā deba ẏe mohora kiriṣāṇa
<P>ẏe mohora upare dekhāucchi chanduāḷa paṇa | 59 |
<P>goḷa śabada śuṇi bijekale yujheṣṭhi
<P>dekhile siṁghadvāre kaṇaẏa jāli goṭi | 60 |
<P>sureśvara boilā deba ẏe mohora kiriṣāṇa
<P>kodāḷa dei boili ẏe budāmāna hāṇa | 61 |
<P>hāṇante tahiṁr̥ pāilā ẏe amūlya ratna nidhi
<P>bho deba ratna ẏehāra hoibanā bidhi | 62 |
<P>ẏeḍe chanduāḷa niki caṣāloka hoi
<P>ẏehāra arajilā dhana ẏe mohora upare pakāi | 63 |
<P1>56|2 rājāra chamuku chāla yibā se bichāra karibe yāhā |(ka)
[MBO-11(3)-7]
<P>yujheṣṭhi debe boile yebe pāilu ratnajāli (jhari)
<P>dhana na nei kimpe brāhmaṇa tule dvanda kari | 64 |
<P>kiriṣāṇa boilā deba muṁ karai bepāra
<P>anna basra baratana hoai sinā mora | 65 |
<P>bhūmire yebaṇahiṁ upujai āẏe
<P>ẏehāṁkar ahoi sinā bichāra debarāẏe | 66 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi boile ho adhe adhe kara
<P>bāṇṭinia dhana tumbhe bichāra āmbhara 67 |
<P>kiriṣāṇa boilā deba tumbhe se dharmarāẏe
<P>mohora beḷete nei nohai cināẏe | 68 |
<P>brāhmaṇa boilā muṁ cināẏe kimpe nebi
<P>ẏehu dukhe arjilā muhiṁ kesane haribi | 69 |
<P>śuṇiṇa āśrija hoile yujheṣṭhi nr̥pabara
<P>sahadebaku boile ẏe kebaṇa bichāra | 70 |
<P>sahadeba boilā deba bujhibā ẏehikṣaṇi
<P>ẏethira tadanta muṁ achainā jāṇi | 71 |
<P>śuṇa deba yujheṣṭhira ẏethira byabasthā
<P>kaḷiyuga prabeśa hoilā śuṇimā tathya kathā | 72 |
<P>udiyoge śrīkr̥ṣṇa hoigale dūta
<P>sehidinuṁ kaḷiyuga hoilā udita | 73 |
<P>hari arjunara bhaẏeṇa paśita nuārilā
<P>mahābhāratha yuddhe kaḷi prabeśa hoilā | 74 |
<P>āmbhara samaẏe sukha bhoga nimante
<P>kaḷiki paśi na dile sahadeba jagannāthe | 75 |
<P1>65|2 kiriṣāṇa boilā muṁ kiṁpe karibi abebhāra |(ḍa)
<P1>69|2 ẏehu dukhe arjilā muṁ kisa karibi |(śa, ḍa, cha)
[MBO-11(3)-8]
<P>ākāśara bāṇī paḍilā śuṇa he sahadeba
<P>anīti paḍibaṭi tumbhe na thāa ẏeba | 76 |
<P>kr̥ṣṇa aile arjuna nāhiṁ svarge
<P>puṇa jāta hoibanā kaḷiyuga bhoge | 77 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi deba ākāśe ye naile nohai
<P>dharmarājā na thile ākāśa na śohai | 78 |
<P>ākāśara bāṇī śuṇi mantrī udabega
<P>kaḷikāḷa phāśi pheidile kaḷiẏaga | 79 |
<P>ẏekā nimiṣake saẏaḷa jaḷa ghoṭi
<P>lāgilā māẏāmoha ghoṭilā nabasr̥ṣṭi | 80 |
<P>sureśara brāhmaṇa boilā ẏe dhana mohora boli
<P>paḷā yāa sādhuta boli kiriṣāṇa dilā peli | 81 |
<P>brāhmaṇa bolai deba tumbhe ye dharmarāẏe
<P>kiriṣāṇa mātra hoi sādhuku baḷa kaẏe | 82 |
<P>brāhmaṇa koḷakri dharai yāiṁ jāri
<P>baḷeṇa kiriṣāṇa ye niāi uchuḍi | 83 |
<P>dekhiṇa yujheṣṭhi nāśikāẏe dile hātha
<P>ẏehikṣaṇi sahadeba re hoilā kemanta | 84 |
<P>sahadeba boilā yeuṁ dinuṁ kr̥ṣṇa dūtapaṇe gale
<P>sehi dinu kaḷiyuga prabeśa hoile | 85 |
<P>mahābhāratha yuddha yahuṁ śeṣa hoilā
<P>mote hakāri deba kr̥ṣṇa ye boilā | 86 |
<P>kāḷeka yujheṣṭhi deba baneṇa mahādukhī
<P>rājakumāra hoi nohile kicchi sukhi | 87 |
<P1>76 tumbhe nathāanti anīti paḍiba
<>anīti paḍibaṭi tumbhe nathiba kaḷiyuga |(cha, ṭa)
<P1>81|1 sureśvara brahmāṇa boilā ẏe mora arjilāra jāli |(ṭa, ṇa)
<P1>82|2 kiriṣāṇa mātra hoi baḷatkāra kaẏe |(jha, cha)
<P1>83|1 jāri = jāla |
[MBO-11(3)-9]
<P>ẏete boli deba kaḷiyuga bandhana kalu āmbhe
<P>samaẏeka sukhabhoga pāila deba tumbhe | 88 |
<P>kaliyuga pheḍante deba hoilā ẏemanta
<P>yujheṣṭhi boile kimpe kaḷiyuga hoiba anitya | 89 |
<P>parīkṣa boile deba pr̥thīre thilā sunā
<P>bichārile yugate ẏe rājāra bhaṇḍāra dhana sinā | 90 |
<P>sādhaba kiriṣāṇa gale mana mr̥cchi
<P>bhaṇḍāre dhana thoile yujheṣṭhi na boile kicchi | 91 |
<P>sahadeba boilā deba śuṇimā sābadhāne
<P>kaḷiyugara carita hoiba ẏemanta bidhāne | 92 |
<P>aneka kaṣṭe parajāẏe upujāibe kr̥ṣi
<P>nāna chanda pāti rājā nema duirāśi | 93 |
<P>yahuṁ se abidhi karibāka rāẏe
<P>indra br̥ṣṭi na kariba pr̥thī nohiba phaḷadāẏe | 94 |
<P>parajā duirāśi na aṇṭiba rājāku
<P>kaṭāḷa karibe se debatā brāhmaṇaṁku | 95 |
<P>rājā hoibe śāguṇā parajā hoibe maḍā
<P>ṭhāba ṭhāba hoi se uṭhibāka paḍā | 96 |
<P>śūdrakaiṁ brāhmaṇe ye māgire taḷahāthe
<P>nityakarma tejibe anna abhyāgate | 97 |
<P>āchāra teji brāhmaṇe hoibe anāchārī
<P>rājasebā karibe ye daṇḍapāṭa ābori | 98 |
<P>kr̥ṣi karmeṇa ye daḷibāka mahī
<P>śahasra dhari śira chedibāka sehi | 99 |
<P>bedamantramāna se ye hoiba agrāhija
<P>brāhmaṇa stirī yonire chāṇḍāḷe debe bīryya | 100 |
<P1>95|2 rājasebā karibe daṇḍapāṭa ācari |(ṭa, ṇa)
[MBO-11(3)-10]
<P>bidhābā brāhmaṇī ye hoibe anyāchāī
<P>kuḷati rīmāne ye hoibe abhisārī | 101 |
<P>bibhāita patnīki karibe upekṣā
<P>bidhabā stirī gheni karibe kuḷa rakṣā | 102 |
<P>bidhāba ramaṇe ye putra hoibāka jāta
<P>pitā mātākaiṁ se nohibe bhagata | 103 |
<P>sukhare strī rati karibe chāri jāti
<P>putra sādhaba pitā mariba anna śāsti | 104 |
<P>śāhāsra nihā karibe kaḷiyuga loke
<P>bhaṇḍapaṇa kari tahiṁ britibe ye thoke | 105 |
<P>kiñchita kathāku kaḷii karibe bahute
<P>dvandeṇa prabartta hoibe pitā putre | 106 |
<P>pitā putra patnīre hoibe ẏeka saṅga
<P>sābata putre mātā hoibe ratiyoga | 107 |
<P>āpaṇāra nija br̥tti chaḍibe śakya hīne
<P>śr̥ṅgāre anyoanyi hoibe hāde jane | 108 |
<P>kaḷira prāntaku ye hoibe ẏekayoga
<P>kaḷiyuge jane pāibe hīnabhoga | 109 |
<P>bāma pūjyajane karibe akīrtti
<P>brāhmaṇa chāṇḍāḷa ye ẏekatve madirā rase arthī | 110 |
<P>svāmīki sebaka ye māribāka beḷe
<P>cauryyakarme bratī hoibe bikate | 111 |
<P>michahuṁ sata jane na kahiba bāṇī
<P>ocha loke siṁghāsane basibe pātra mantrī jāṇi | 112 |
<P1>108|2 hiṁsāre anyoanyi maribāka jane |(tha)
<P1>110|1 bāmapūjā kari pāibe akīrtti |(ḍa)
<P1>110|1 brāhmaṇa chāṇḍāḷa ye madirā arthe māti |(ṇa)
<P1>111|1 cauryyapaṇe prabartti hoibe sakaḷe |(cha)

<>rājāṅkara mukti@}
<P>baibasuta muni agastiṁki kale pūjā
<P>hemabanta parbata upare uṭhile yujheṣṭhi mahārājā | 1 |
<P>debatāmānaṁku dekhile se yebe

<P>japamantra śāsra muṁ na jāṇai kicchi
<P>ẏesaneka āgyāṁ mote dileka kāmākṣī | 105 |
<P>he budhajane jambodīpa bhrathakhaṇḍa oḍarāṣṭa maṇḍaḷe
<P>ṭhāba kaṇaẏābratī nagra candrabhāgā nadīkūḷe | 106 |
<P>mahodadhi uttara taṭe praśurāmaṁka pāṭaṇā
<P>praśurāma pūjākale yebaṇa pratima | 107 |
<P>pratakṣe bhābānī sehi śrīcaṇḍī sāraḷe
<P>se mora tuḷasīmāḷā hoi luḷu bakṣasthaḷe | 108 |
<P>he paṇḍita jane prasanna hoile piṅgaḷā
<P>se sarbamaṅgaḷā hr̥de mora hārā | 109 |

<P>ẏethu anantare bilaṁka deśa rājā
<P>agastiṁka caraṇe kalā dibya pūjā | 1 |

<P>samāpta

<P>sahadeba mūkharu śuṇa śrī mahābhāratha
<P>sakaḷa pāparu tuhi hoibu mukata | 1 |
<P>ẏehi kāmanāre śrī mahābhāratha śuṇa
<P>putra jātra heba tora kuḷa uddhāraṇa | 2 |
<P>pāṇḍaba saṅgare se tora saṅga yeṇu
<P>ẏe nagra loke pāparu taribeṭi teṇu | 3 |
<P>mahāprabhma padmamukhuṁ śuṇiacchi muhiṁ
<P>padmapurāṇa boliṇa śrīhastare lihi | 4 |
<P>bidhātāra hāthe nei dile daẏānidhi

<P>purāṇa madhyare śrīmahābhāratha sāra
<P>debaṁkara deba ẏehu gyāna gyānīṁkara | 6 |
<P>śrīmahabhāratha ye śrabaṇe śuṇai
<P>śatejanma pāpa tāra kṣaṇake nāśa yāi | 7 |
<P>ye abā śrīmahābhāratha kare uccāraṇa
<P>śrotāhuṁ adhika se tāhāra sadaguṇa | 8 |
<P>ādyaprānta kariṇa citta nirmaḷe śuṇiba
<P>ẏekamana hoiṇa saṁśaẏe na kariba | 9 |
<P>dhūpa dīpa naibidya nabīna basana
<P>purāṇa pustaka pūjā kariba hr̥ṣṭamana | 10 |
<P>brahmaṁku nabīna bastra gandha puṣya dei
<P>pādāsana dei tāṁku santoṣa karāi | 11 |
[MBO-11(3)-102]

[MBO-11(3)-129]
<P>kaiḷāsa parbata kare upāḍiṇa datua

[MBO-11(3)-130]
<P>kumāra kumārīṁki bibhā tahiṁ kale

[MBO-11(3)-131]

[MBO-11(3)-132]

<P>tinidina sāṁgrāmare samasta nipātile | 1126 |

<P>āja muṁ pāṇḍabanta saṁhāribi boilā | 1130 |

<P>ẏe bhaba saṁsāre ye utapatti praḷaẏe
<P>puṇi utapatti hoiba galeka samaẏe | 1864 |
<P>ẏeteka āgyāṁ dei galeka nirākāra
<P>tahuṁ bimāne basāile yujheṣṭhi nr̥pabara | 1865 |
[MBO-11(3)-235]
<P>bāsabara putramāne cauṣaṭhi koṭi
<P>udaṇḍa ẏekalakṣī pāṭachatra khaṭi | 1866 |
<P>amar agaṇamāne karanti śaṅkhadhvanī
<P>beda ādhyāna karanti sakaḷa sura muni | 1867 |
<P>amara bidyādhara cauṣathi koṭi
<P>nr̥tyaraṅge ārambhe semāne ye khaṭi | 1868 |
<P>tāḷa marddaḷa pañchaśvara saptaśvara bīṇā
<P>adhāṭi sarahaguṇā haraṣe gāẏeṇā | 1869 |
<P>caḷai bimāna ye sadhīre sadhīre
<P>āgare ratna br̥ṣṭi karanti kubere | 1870 |
<P>hari hari ḍāka tahiṁ paḍai apāra
<P>kusuma br̥ṣṭi tahiṁ karanti sunāśīra | 1871 |
<P>bijighoṣa ṭamaka marddaḷa dundubhi
<P>gamanteṇa śobhābana ye diśuacchi dibi | 1872 |
<P>dharmara nandana ye gamanti śūnyapathe
<P>jaẏa jaẏa dhvani tahiṁ karanti samaste | 1873 |
<P>kehu khadī chāmara kehu ālaṭa dhari biñchi
<P>nandana bana kusuma mārgeṇa nei biñchi | 1874 |
<P>śrīkare bidyādharī gheniṇa arghathāḷī
<P>sānande sura nārakāẏe dianti huḷahuḷi | 1875 |
<P>yāna bāhāna ārohi tetiśa deba koṭi
<P>sānande debatāmāne karanti puṣpa br̥ṣṭi | 1876 |
<P>dharmara nandana ye gamante śohai
<P>prasanna abatāra se jagujana mohai | 1877 |
<P>amar asabhāre bijaẏe yujheṣṭhi rājadebe
<P>samasta draśana kale dharmaṁkara pāẏe | 1878 |
<P>samodra manthana karibā kāḷe
<P>amr̥ta āpyāne bratanti sakaḷa digapāḷe | 1879 |
[MBO-11(3)-236]
<P>bihantā puruṣamāne āsthāna gale chaḍi
<P>basile dharma nandana amara sabhā māḍi | 1880 |
<P>ẏemanta samaẏe nakuḷa sahadeba
<P>āsthāna taḷe bijaẏe chāri ye pāṇḍaba | 1881 |
<P>āsthāne dharmasute sambhāre bijaẏe
<P>amaḷāna basra pinddha amr̥ta pāna kāẏe | 1882 |
<P>pārijātaka kusuma hr̥daẏeṇa kari hāra
<P>śrīkhaṇḍi gandana se lepana hr̥daẏara | 1883 |
<P>sākṣāte dharma rūpe bijaẏe yujheṣṭhira
<P>chāri bhrāthaṁku dekhile se āsthāna taḷara | 1884 |
<P>bhīma arjuna nakuḷa sahadeba sāna
<P>ẏeṁhāku dekhi haraṣa yujheṣṭhi rājana | 1885 |
<P>śuṇa baibasuta manu agasti kahile
<P>driyodhana śate bhrāthāṁku yujheṣṭhi dekhile | 1886 |
<P>pannagā nāraẏaṇa bijaẏe āsthānare
<P>śate bhrātha khaṭichanti āsthāna taḷara | 1887 |
<P>bhīṣma droṇa śalya ye śaṁkūni
<P>basile amare se nakṣatra rūpa gheni | 1888 |
<P>mahābhāratha yuddhe paḍile yete jana
<P>sate nisate hoile amara bhmabana | 1889 |
<P>sañjaẏe lakṣmaṇakumara abhimanyu
<P>pañchāḷa kumar aghaṭitkaca aḷambuṣa tanu | 1890 |
<P>birāṭa dropada ye śaṅkha śveta uttara
<P>śikhaṇḍī dhr̥ṣṭadr̥mana aneka nr̥pabara | 1891 |
<P>lakṣeka rajane ye dekhile dharmabacche
<P>ẏekāmātra dhr̥tirāṣṭakaiṁ na dekhi pratakṣe | 1892 |
<P>kuru pāṇḍaba samara yete kale ohobaḷa sanya gheni
<P>lakṣe rājāra yeteka paḍile saini | 1893 |
[MBO-11(3)-237]
<P>mr̥tyu maṇḍaḷe yehne hoile ātajāta
<P>sehi svarge svarūpe basile samasta | 1894 |
<P>śuṇa baibasuta manu hoile agasti
<P>arjunara bhābāni se subhadrā puṣpabatī | 1895 |
<P>hārābatīki pātha hoile pradāma
<P>nikumbha daitaku kariṇa nidhana | 1896 |
<P>pātāḷe bibhā helā ananta nandinī
<P>nāgārjjuna kumarara aṭai jananī | 1897 |
<P>bhīmasenara bhārijā aṭai belābāḷī
<P>hiḍambeka bane prabeśa hoile mahābaḷī | 1898 |
<P>hiḍimbikī rākṣasīki pradāna hoile
<P>ghaṭotkaṭa tāra nandana upujile | 1899 |
<P>yujheṣṭhira pradāna hoile suhāṇī nāme kanyā | 1900 |
<P>aneḷe dāha hele ẏehu sarba bāmā
<P>ẏemāne sage yāi samaste basile
<P>ye yāhāra svāmī saṅge niścinte rahile | 1901 |
<P>puṇi kicchi samaẏeke marttyare hebe janma
<P>ẏehi rūpe beḷe beḷe bhāratha sāṁgrāma | 1902 |
<P>śuṇa he sugyaṁjane mahābharatha puṇyagati
<P>paḍhante śuṇante ẏehirūpe labhiba svarga gati | 1903 |
<P>śrīmahābhāratha ẏe amr̥ta rasabāṇī
<P>pāpādhi mahapāpa khaṇḍanti catrapāṇi | 1904 |
<P>aputrika jane ye pābanti pūtra gati
<P>amukhya prāṇimāne pāibe sadagati | 1905 |
<P>dharma artha kāma mokṣa yāhāra yisa icchā
<P>śrī mahābhāratha ẏe biṣṇura purāṇa
<P>śrabaṇe śuṇile patita nistāraṇa | 1907 |
[MBO-11(3)-238]
<P>kebaḷa dakṣiṇā ye deba mana pūrṇṇa
<P>baka tāku maṇiba byāsaṁka samāna | 1908 |
<P>dhūpa dīpa deiṇa naibedya pūjākara
<P>dakṣiṇā nadile karṇṇa hoai badhīra | 1909 |
<P>ẏemanta prakāre ye kahile agasti
<P>śuṇiṇa mahāsantoṣa bilaṁka adhipati | 1910 |
<P>lakṣeka ratna dei mūniṁki kale pūjā
<P>āpaṇe brahmaloka caḷile brahma dvājā | 1911 |
<P>namaste nārāẏaṇa patita paritrāṇa
<P>namaste nārāẏaṇa he kamaḷā ramaṇa | 1912 |
<P>namaste nārāẏaṇa he paṅkaja locana
<P>namaste nārāẏaṇa śrībaccha lāñcchana | 1913 |
<P>namaste nārāẏaṇa sakaḷe bhūte bāsa
<P>namaste nārāẏaṇa he pradhāna puruṣa | 1914 |
<P>namaste nārāẏaṇa nabīnaghana bapu
<P>namaste bidārila he hiraṇya kaśipu | 1915 |
<P>namaste nārāẏaṇa he saẏaḷajana sañchā
<P>namaste nārāẏaṇa he akāḷa kāma bāñcchā | 1916 |
<P>namaste nārāẏaṇa ye kare tote dhyāna
<P>niścante basanti se ye baikuṇṭha bhmabana | 1917 |
<P>namaste nārāẏaṇa danuja niśodhana
<P>śūdramuni sāroḷā dāsaku karibā kāraṇa | 1918 |
